(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing
         sharpObject - object
         microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co))
)

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing
         sharpObject - object
         microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co))
)

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing
         sharpObject - object
         microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r))
    :effect (sliced ?co))
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)

               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)

               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)

               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r) (isSharp ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)))

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r) (isSharp ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)))

  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r) (isSharp ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)))

  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)

               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
               (isClosable ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)) (isClosable ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isClosable ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r) (isSharp ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)))

(define (domain exploration_domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object - thing)
  (:predicates (at ?r - receptacle)
               (opened ?r - receptacle)
               (holding ?o - object)
               (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
               (visited ?r - receptacle)
               (used ?o - object)
               (heated ?o - object)
               (cleaned ?o - object)
               (cooled ?o - object)
               (sliced ?o - object)
               (isSharp ?o - object)
               (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
               (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
               (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
               (isClosable ?r - receptacle))
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to)))
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)) (isClosable ?r))
    :effect (opened ?r))
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isClosable ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r)))
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r))))
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (in ?o ?r)))
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o))
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o))
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o))
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (opened ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o))
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (opened ?r) (isSharp ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)))
